* The first implementation of the GameZIP system is complete. Some file-heavy games now come packed in ZIP format for a reduction in overall file count in Flashpoint Ultimate. This feature is currently in beta; around 130 games have been zipped so far. Infinity does not utilize this system due to a lack of time; it'll be integrated into Infinity come a later version.

* The Launcher has seen various updates which can be explored in full at https://gist.github.com/colin969/3b0237d614c23b5a8945169e246796cb - but here's a quick summary:
 * The launcher now has an Extensions system. We're not making use of it in this release.
 * Extreme games now have a secondary logo that displays in the launcher.
 * Extreme playlists can now be made, which will be hidden in .
 * There are now Logo Sets, which can be set independently or with themes.
 * On Demand Images no longer causes Flashpoint to not work with no internet connection.
 * Playlists should now display properly with no duplicate entries.
 * The Logs tab should now display new lines better.
 * More technical aspects we won't talk about just yet.

* Newgrounds Auditorium has been removed from Infinity; it was originally meant as a launcher stress test, and as such has served its purpose. You can still access it with a copy of 8.2 Infinity, or download the standalone from https://bluemaxima.org/auditorium. We're hoping to upload a new build with a fixed launcher sometime in the near future.
